The Trustee will establish (i) separate subaccounts in the Interest Subfund and Principal 
Subfund of the Debt Service Fund for each Series of Bonds, (ii) separate subaccounts in the Debt 
Service Reserve Fund for any and each Series of Bonds to which the Debt Service Reserve Fund 
applies, (iii) separate subaccounts in the Construction Fund for each Series of Bonds with 
proceeds required to be deposited in the Construction Fund. 
The Revenue Fund and the Subfunds therei n, the Contingency Fund and the Rate 
Stabilization Fund each w ill be held by the City and not commingled with other moneys of the 
City except for purposes of investment.  The Debt Service Fund, Debt Service Reserve Fund, 
Construction Fund and Rebate Fund each will be held by the Trustee.  The Subordinated Debt 
Service Fund will be held by the City or by the Trustee or such trustee or  other party as may be 
specified in the trust agreement or other contract  between the City and the holder or holders of 
the Subordinated Indebtedness.  All moneys or securities deposited with the Trustee pursuant to 
the Trust Agreement will be held in trust and ap plied only in accordance with the provisions of 
the Trust Agreement and will be considered trust funds for the purposes of the Trust Agreement.  
B-16 
Construction Fund 
There will be deposited from time to time in the Construction Fund the portion of the 
proceeds of the Bonds required to be deposited therein by any Supplemental Bond Ordinance 
and Supplemental Trust Agreement.  Amounts in the Construction Fund will be expended only 
to pay Capital Costs and Costs of Issuance or to cure any deficiency in the Debt Service Fund or 
the Debt Service Reserve Fund following the de posits required, as described under “Revenue 
Fund,” which follows. 
Revenue Fund 
The City is required to cause a ll cash receipts that constitute Revenues of the System to 
be deposited into the Revenue Fund, along with any amounts that the City elects to transfer to the 
Revenue Fund from the Rate Stabilization Fund.  The amounts in the Revenue Fund will be 
deposited in the Operating Subfund and first a pplied to the payment of Operating Expenses; 
thereafter, the balance in the Revenue Fund up to the Working Cap ital Reserve will be deposited 
in the Working Capital Reserve Subfund and retained as a reserve for the payment of Operating 
Expenses and used for that purpose if the Oper ating Subfund will have been fully expended; and 
thereafter, the balance in the Revenue Fund will be paid at the times and in the amounts as 
follows: 
(A) To the Trustee for deposit in the Debt Service Fund as follows: 
            1. Monthly, on or before the last day of each month, the City will pay to the 
Trustee, for deposit in each subaccount in the Interest Subfund in the Debt Service Fund, an 
amount equal to one-sixth of the amount of interest due on the next Interest Payment Date on the 
Outstanding Bonds of the Series to which such subaccount relates; provided, however, that if 
fewer than six months precede the next Interest Payment Date, then, on or before the last day of 
each such month an amount that, if deposited in each such m onth, would equal the amount of 
interest due on the next Interest Payment Date on the Outstanding Bonds of the Series to which 
such subaccount relates will be deposited therein; provided furt her, however, such monthly 
payments need be made only to the extent that the amount then on deposit in any such 
subaccount is less than the amount required to be  on deposit therein in a ccordance herewith; and 
provided yet further, however, that the frequenc y and amount of any deposits required by this 
paragraph will be subject to adjustment pursu ant to the requirements of the General Bond 
Ordinance to make the deposits required for any Se ries of Bonds or any Parity Swap Obligations 
no less frequent than those for any other Series. 
            2. Monthly, on or before the last day of each of the twelve months that 
precede a month in which a Serial Maturity Date occurs or a Sinking Fund Installment is due, the 
City will pay to the Trustee for deposit in each applicable subaccount in the Principal Subfund in 
the Debt Service Fund an amount equal to one-twelfth of the amount necessary to provide for the 
payment of the principal due on the next Serial  Maturity Date or of the next Sinking Fund 
Installment; provided, however, th at if fewer than twelve mont hs precede the next month in 
which a Serial Maturity Date occurs or a Sinking Fund Installm ent is due, then, on or before the 
last day of each such month an amount that, if deposited in ea ch such month, would equal the 
amount of principal due on the next Serial Maturity Date or of the next Sinking Fund Installment 
for the Outstanding Bonds of the Series to wh ich such subaccount relates will be deposited  
B-17 
therein; provided further, however, such monthly payments need be made only to the extent that 
the amount then on deposit in any such subaccount  is less than the amount required to be on 
deposit therein in accordance here with; and provided yet further, however, that the frequency 
and amount of any deposits required by this paragr aph will be subject to adjustment pursuant to 
the requirements of the General Bond Ordinance to  make the deposits required for any Series of 
Bonds or any Parity Swap Obligations no less frequent than those for any other Series. 
(B) To the Trustee for deposit in the Debt Service Reserve Fund, monthly on or 
before the last day of each month, commenci ng on the date set forth in the applicable 
Supplemental Bond Ordinance with respect to any Series of Bonds for which the Debt Service 
Reserve Requirement is to be de posited in the Debt Service Rese rve Fund, the City must pay to 
the Trustee for deposit in the suba ccount established in the Debt Service Reserve Fund for such 
Series of Additional Bonds, an amount such that, if that same amount were deposited in equal 
monthly installments, the aggregate of the amou nts so deposited in such subaccount would be 
equal to the Debt Service Reserv e Requirement with respect to su ch Series of Additional Bonds 
on the fifth (5th) anniversary of such commence ment date, after giving effect to any amounts 
already on deposit therein and pledged to such Se ries of Additional Bonds .  Thereafter, if the 
amount on deposit in such subaccount at any tim e is less than the Debt Service Reserve 
Requirement with respect to such Series of Add itional Bonds, the City must pay to the Trustee 
for deposit in such subaccount, on or the before the last day of each mont h following the date of 
such deficiency, an amount equal to one-twelfth of such defici ency.  The frequency and amount 
of any deposits required by this pa ragraph will be subject to adju stment pursuant to the General 
Bond Ordinance so that the deposits required by the provisions summarized by this paragraph for 
any Series of Bonds will be no less frequent th an the deposits required by paragraph (A) above 
for Bond Service Charges or Parity Swap Obligations. 
(C) To any custodians of the Subordinated Debt Service Fund for deposit therein, 
such amounts as are required to be deposited therein on such dates as are specified in the 
Supplemental Trust Agreement or other contracts between the City and the holder or holders of 
the Subordinated Indebtedness.  If any Supplemen tal Trust Agreement or other contract between 
the City and the holder or holders of Subordina ted Indebtedness requires the establishment and 
funding a reserve account related to such Subordinated Indebtedness, then any required deposits 
to such reserve account may be  made after any otherwise requi red deposits described by this 
paragraph (C) but before any required deposits described under paragraphs (D) and (E), below. 
(D) To the Contingency Fund, monthly on or before the last day of each month on 
which the balance in the Contingency Fund is less than the Contingency Fund Requirement, not 
less than 1/12 of the amount by which the Contingency Fund Requirement exceeds the balance. 
(E) To the Rate Stabilization Fund, on any date on which deposits are required to be 
made by the provisions described in paragraphs (A) through (D), above, and after all such 
deposits are made, any amounts that the City elects to make to the Rate Stabilization Fund. 
(F) On the first day of each Fi scal Year or on the first prac ticable date thereafter, the 
City will deposit any balance remaining in th e Operating Subfund and the Working Capital 
Reserve Subfund in excess of the Working Capital Reserve at the end of the preceding Fiscal 
Year to the credit of the Balance Subfund; provi ded, that the City may at any time provide for 
semiannual or quarterly deposits of such Net Revenues to the Balance Subfund.  
B-18 
(G) Upon receipt of any Direct Payment, th e City or the Truste e will cause it to be 
deposited (i) in the appropriate subaccount in the Debt Service Fund if such Direct Payment 
relates to Bonds, and (ii)  in the appropriate account in the Subordinated Debt Service Fund if 
such Direct Payment relates to Subordinated Inde btedness, and will cause it to be applied solely 
to the purposes to which the Trust Agreement permits funds in such subaccount and account to 
be applied. 
Debt Service Fund 
The Trustee will pay out of the applicable subaccounts in the Interest Subfund and in the 
Principal Subfund in the applicable Debt Servic e Fund to each Paying Agent (i) on or before 
each Interest Payment Date for the Bonds of each Series (x) the amount required for the interest 
payable on all such Outstanding Bonds on such date  and (y) the amount, if any, required for the 
payment of the principal maturing on all such Outstanding Bonds on such date, and (ii) on or 
before the day preceding the redemption date for any such Bonds to be redeemed at the option of 
the City, the amount required for the payment of  such Bonds then to be redeemed.  Such 
amounts will be so applied by each Paying Agent on and after the due date thereof. 
The City will pay to the Trustee for deposit in  the Debt Service Fund any moneys held in 
any other Funds or Subfunds in excess of the amount s required to be mainta ined therein that the 
City has elected to apply to the redemption prior to maturity of any Bonds, and such amounts 
will be so applied by the Trustee in the manner and at the times provided in the Trust Agreement. 
Amounts in the applicable subaccount in the Principal Subfund for the payment of any 
Sinking Fund Installment for the Term Bonds of any Series then Outstanding (together with 
amounts in the applicable subaccount in the Intere st Subfund with respect to the Term Bonds for 
which such Sinking Fund Installm ent was established) will be applied by the Trustee to the 
redemption of Term Bonds of th e Series and maturity for whic h such Sinking Fund Installment 
was established in an amount not exceeding that necessary to effect the mandatory redemption of 
such Term Bonds on the Mandatory Redemption Da tes.  The Trustee will, by giving notice as 
provided in the Trust Agreement, proceed to ca ll for redemption on the due date of any such 
Sinking Fund Installment the Term Bonds of the Series and maturity fo r which such Sinking 
Fund Installment was established (except in the case of Term Bonds maturing on a Sinking Fund 
Installment date), in such amount as will be n ecessary to effect the mandatory redemption of 
such Term Bonds on the Mandatory Redemption Date  in an amount equal to the amount of such 
Sinking Fund Installment.  The principal amount of  Term Bonds of such Series and maturity 
theretofore delivered by the City  to the Trustee to satisfy such  Sinking Fund Installment, in the 
manner and to the extent as may be provided for in the General Bond Ordinance or in the 
Supplemental Bond Ordinance or Supplemental Tr ust Agreement authoriz ing such Series, will 
be credited against the amount of such Sinking Fund Installment.  Such notice will be given 
regardless of whether or not moneys therefor wi ll have been deposited in the Principal Subfund 
in the applicable Debt Service Fund and without a ny instructions of the C ity.  The Trustee will 
pay out of the Principal Subfund in the applicable  Debt Service Fund to the appropriate Paying 
Agent, on or before the day preceding such Mandatory Redemption Date, the amount required 
for the redemption of the Term Bonds so called for redemption, and such amount will be applied 
by such Paying Agent to such redemption.  All e xpenses in connection with such redemption of 
Term Bonds will be paid by the City from the Operating Subfund.  
B-19 
To the extent that a Series of Bonds is secured by credit enhancement or liquidity support 
provided by a Credit Provider pursuant to a Re imbursement Agreement, the Supplemental Bond 
Ordinance and Supplemental Trust Agreement with respect to that  Series may provide that the 
Trustee will apply amounts in the Debt Servic e Fund first, to the payment of Bond Service 
Charges and any Parity Swap Obligations then  due and, second, to the payment of any Credit 
Obligations then due. 
Debt Service Reserve Fund 
If on any Interest Payment Date, the amount in  the subaccount in the Interest Subfund or 
the Principal Subfund for any Seri es of Bonds is less than the amount required to be therein on 
deposit pursuant to the Trust Agreement, the Trustee will, after any required deposits to 
Subordinated Debt Service F und, Contingency Fund, Rate Stab ilization Fund and Balance 
Subfund are made, apply the amounts in the app licable Subfund, if any, in the Debt Service 
Reserve Fund to the extent necessary to make good any such deficiency (or the entire amount in 
the applicable Subfund if less than sufficient).  The City may, so long as it will not result in a 
reduction of the rating assigned to any of the B onds, substitute for funds on deposit in the Debt 
Service Reserve Fund a letter of credit, surety bond or other credit enhancement facility issued 
by a Qualified Financial Institution. 
Subordinated Debt Service Fund 
If on the third day before any Interest Paym ent Date, the amount in  any of the Subfunds 
in the Debt Service Fund is less than the amount required to be on deposit therein pursuant to the 
General Bond Ordinance, after deposits, if any, are made to the Contingency Fund, Rate 
Stabilization Fund and Balance S ubfund, the City will, upon the request  of the Trustee, transfer 
or cause the transfer of moneys from the Subordinated Debt Service Fund to the Trustee to make 
good any such deficiency (or the entire amount in the Subordinate d Debt Service Fund if less 
than sufficient). 
If on any day next following the date of a payment and deposit re quired into a Debt 
Service Reserve Fund, the amount in any of the Subfunds in the Debt Service Reserve Fund is 
less than the amount required to be on deposit therein, the City will, upon the request of the 
Trustee, transfer moneys from the Subordinated Debt Service Fund to the Trustee for deposit in 
the appropriate Subfund in the Debt Service Reserve Fund an amount sufficient to cure any such 
deficiency (or the entire amount in the Subordinated Debt Service Fund if less than sufficient). 
Subject to the provisions relating to the Rebate Fund, the amounts on deposit in the 
Subordinated Debt Service Fund will be applied to the payment of the principal of and interest 
and any premium on Subordinated I ndebtedness as and when due or  to the requir ed funding of 
any special reserve account established for any Subordinated Indebtedness. 
Contingency Fund 
If on the third day before any Interest Paym ent Date, the amount in  any of the Subfunds 
in the Debt Service Fund is less than the amount required to be on deposit therein pursuant to the 
General Bond Ordinance, after deposits, if any, are made to the Rate Stabilization Fund and the 
Balance Subfund, the City will, upon the request of th e Trustee, transfer or cause the transfer of  
B-20 
moneys from the Contingency Fund to the Trustee to the extent necessary to make good any such 
deficiency (or the entire amount in the Contingency Fund if less than sufficient). 
If on any day next following the date of a payment and deposit required into the Debt 
Service Reserve Fund, the amount in any of the Subfunds in the Debt Service Reserve Fund is 
less than the amount required to be on deposit therein pursuant to the Ge neral Bond Ordinance, 
the City will, upon the request of the Trustee, tr ansfer moneys from the Contingency Fund to the 
Trustee for deposit in the appropriate Subfund in the Debt Service Reserve Fund an amount 
sufficient to cure any such defi ciency (or the entire amount in the Contingency Fund if less than 
sufficient). 
Subject to the provisions described in the two proceeding paragraphs and the 
requirements of the General Bond Ordinance pe rtaining to the Rebate Fund, the amounts on 
deposit in the Contingency Fund may be used only  for the payment of Capital Costs or for the 
purpose of redeeming Bonds. 
Rate Stabilization Fund 
If on the third day before any Interest Paym ent Date, the amount in  any of the Subfunds 
in the Debt Service Fund is less than the amount required to be on deposit therein pursuant to the 
General Bond Ordinance, after deposits, if any,  are made from the Balance Subfund, the City 
will, upon the request of the Trust ee, transfer or cause the transf er of moneys from the Rate 
Stabilization Fund to the Trustee to make good any such deficiency  (or the entire amount in the 
Rate Stabilization Fund if less than sufficient). 
If on any day next following the date of a payment and deposit required into the Debt 
Service Reserve Fund, the amount in any of the Subfunds in the Debt Service Reserve Fund is 
less than the amount required to be on deposit, the City will, upon the request of the Trustee, 
transfer moneys from the Rate Stabilization F und to the Trustee for deposit in the appropriate 
Subfund in the Debt Service Reserve Fund an amount  sufficient to cure any such deficiency (or 
the entire amount in the Rate Stabilization Fund if less than sufficient). 
Subject to the provisions of described in the two preceding paragraphs, the City may 
from time to time transfer amounts on deposit in  the Rate Stabilization Fund to the Revenue 
Fund and cause them to be applied as Revenues. 
Balance Subfund 
If on the third day before any Interest Paym ent Date, the amount in  any of the Subfunds 
in the Debt Service Fund is less than the amount required to be on deposit in that fund, the City 
will, upon the request of the Trustee, transfer moneys from the Balance Subfund to the Trustee to 
make good any such deficiency (o r the entire amount in  the Subordinated De bt Service Fund if 
less than sufficient). 
If on any day next following a payment date, the amount in any of the Subfunds in the 
Debt Service Reserve Fund is less than the amo unt required to be on deposit in that fund, the 
City will, upon the request of the Trustee, transfer moneys from the Balance Subfund to the 
Trustee for deposit in the appropriate Subfund in the Debt Service Reserve Fund an amount  
B-21 
sufficient to cure any such defi ciency (or the entire amount in the Balance Subf und if less than 
sufficient). 
Subject to the provisions described in the two immediately preceding paragraphs and the 
provisions described in the discussion of the Rebate Fund, below, the amounts on deposit in the 
Balance Subfund will be applied by the City to a ny lawful System purposes, including, but not 
limited to, transfers to the Subordinated Debt Se rvice Fund for payment of  the principal of and 
interest on any Subordinated I ndebtedness and the funding or replenishment of any special 
reserve account es tablished for any Subordinated Indebt edness, but amounts on deposit in the 
Balance Subfund may not be transferred or credited to the Rate Stabilization Fund. 
Rebate Fund 
The General Bond Ordinance establishes and or ders to be maintain ed as a separate 
deposit account (except when inve sted) in the custody of the Trustee a Reba te Fund.  Any 
provision of the General Bond Ordinance or of the Trust Agreement to the contrary 
notwithstanding, the Rebate Fund is not pledged to  the payment of Bond Service Charges, is not 
one of or part of any of the Special Funds, a nd is free and clear of any lien of the Trust 
Agreement.  Separate accounts will be created in the Rebate Fund for each Series of Bonds, 
commencing with the Series 2016 Bonds. 
At least five days prior to the end of the fifth Bond Year and each fifth Bond Year 
thereafter for each Series of Bonds, including th e Series 2016 Bonds, and within five days after 
the date on which al l outstanding Bonds of such Series are pa id or deemed paid in full, the City 
will calculate or will furnish information to  and engage an independent certified public 
accounting firm that is not unacceptable to the Trustee, to calculate, the Rebate Amount as of the 
end of that Bond Year or the date of such final payment.  The Tr ustee may rely upon the City for 
the calculation of the Rebate Amount, provided that the Trustee receives  a verification of the 
accuracy of such computations by a firm of independent certif ied public accountants or an 
opinion of nationally recognized bond counsel that such computations are in compliance with the 
Code.  Within 30 days after the end of the fift h Bond Year and every fift h Bond Year thereafter, 
the Trustee, acting on behalf of the City and at the written direction of the City, will pay to the 
United States in accordance with Section 148(f) of  the Code from the moneys then on deposit in 
the applicable account in the Rebate Fund an amount equal to 90% (or such greater percentage 
not in excess of 100% as the City may direct the Trustee in writing to pay) of the Rebate Amount 
determined from the date of the original delivery  of the Bonds of that Se ries (less the portion of 
the Rebate Amount, if any, previously paid to the United States).  Within sixty (60) days after the 
payment in full of all outstandi ng Bonds of such Series and upon written direction of the City, 
the Trustee will pay to the United States in acco rdance with Section 148(f) of the Code from the 
moneys then on deposit in the applicable account in the Rebate  Fund an amount equal to 100% 
of the Rebate Amount determined from the date of the original delivery of the Bonds of that 
Series to the date of such payment (but less that portion of the Rebate Amount, if any, previously 
paid to the United States) and any moneys remaining in the applicable  account in the Rebate 
Fund following such payment will be  paid to the City.  Notwithstan ding anything in the General 
Bond Ordinance to the contrary, the moneys needed for any payment required by the preceding 
two sentences may be derived from balances in any of the Special Funds other than the Debt 
Service Fund and the Debt Service Reserve Fund, and the City agrees  to apply those balances to 
that purpose in the following Order: the Ba lance Subfund, the Rate Stabilization Fund, the  
B-22 
Contingency Fund, the Subordinated Indebtedness Fund and any related reserve fund or account, 
and the Construction Fund. 
Investment of Funds and Subfunds 
Moneys held in the Debt Service Reserv e Fund or in any speci al reserve account 
established for any Series of Bonds will be inve sted and reinvested, in  accordance with written 
instructions received from the C ity, by the Trustee, to the fullest extent practicable, in Eligible 
Investments maturing not later than the final ma turity of the Series of Bonds for which the 
applicable subaccount was established or subject to withdrawal at any time required for purposes 
of the Debt Service Reserve Fund. 
Moneys held in the Debt Service Fund will be  invested and reinvested, in accordance 
with written instructions from th e City, by the Trustee, to the fullest extent possible, in Eligible 
Investments maturing within one year from the date of purchase but in any event not later than 
such times as is necessary to provide moneys for required payments to be made from such Funds 
or subject to withdrawal at any such time. 
Except as otherwise provided in the Gene ral Bond Ordinance with respect to the 
investment of moneys in the Debt Service Fund and the Debt Service Reserve Fund or any 
special reserve account established for any Series  of Bonds, and only to the extent otherwise 
provided, moneys held in the Funds and Subfunds  are invested and reinvested by the City and 
the Trustee, as the case may be, to the fullest extent practicable, in Eligible Investments that 
mature or are subject to withdrawal not later than  such times as are necessary to provide moneys 
for payments to be made from such Funds and Subfunds, as required by the General Bond 
Ordinance and in the applicable Supplemen tal Bond Ordinance or Supplemental Trust 
Agreement; provided, however, that  the Trustee may make such i nvestments only in accordance 
with instructions received from the City. 
An investment that can be redeemed at the op tion of the holder or th at may be sold at a 
pre-established price to a “Qualified Purchase  Agreement Provider” (as hereinafter defined) 
pursuant to a written agreement within a specified  time period will be deemed to mature within 
that specified time period for purposes of lim itations in the General Bond Ordinance on the 
maximum maturity of investments, but only for as  long as the redemption or sale option remains 
exercisable within the specified period.  A “Q ualified Purchase Agreement Provider” means a 
financial institution, including, without limitation, a bank (including the Trustee or any of its 
affiliates) or insurance company) that is rated, or the obligations of which are rated, in one of the 
top two rating categories by at least two Rating Agencies. 
In computing the amount in any Fund or Subfund established under th e provisions of the 
General Bond Ordinance, obligations purchased as an investment of moneys therein will be 
valued at the lower of market value or the amorti zed value thereof.  Amortized value, when used 
with respect to an obligation purchased at par,  means the par amount thereof, and, when used 
with respect to an obligation purchased at a pr emium above or a discount below par, means the 
value as of any given time obtained by dividing the total premium or discount at which such 
obligation was purchased by the nu mber of interest payments re maining on such obligation after 
such purchase and deducting the amount thus calculated for each interest payment date after such 
purchase from the purchase price in the case of an obligation purchased at a premium and adding  
B-23 
the amount thus calculated for ea ch interest payment date after such purchase to the purchase 
price in the case of an obligation purchased at a discount. 
Except as otherwise provided in the General Bond Ordinance, the Trustee will sell at the 
best price obtainable, using reasonable diligence to determine such best price, or present for 
redemption, any obligation so purchased as an investment whenever it is so requested in writing 
by the Director of Finance or whenever it is necessary in order to provide moneys to meet any 
payment or transfer from any Fund held by it. 
Investments purchased as an investment of moneys in any Fund or Subfund will be 
deemed at all times to be a part of such Fund or Subfund, and any losses suffered due to the 
investment thereof will be charged to such Fund  or Subfund.  A deficiency in a Subfund in the 
Debt Service Reserve Fund will not be deemed to ex ist as of a date of transfer if the amount on 
deposit therein is less than the applicable Debt  Service Reserve Requirement with respect to any 
Series of Bonds solely because as of such date of transfer one or more deposits to such Subfund 
in the Debt Service Reserve Fund is not required in connection with the original issuance of such 
Series until a future date or dates. 
The valuation and sale of investments may be amended in the Master Trust Agreement or 
any Supplemental Trust Agreement upon the request of a Credit Provider. 
Authorization of the Issuance of Bonds 
The Trust Agreement authorizes the issuance from time to time of Bonds for the purpose 
only of paying Capital Costs, or refunding, includ ing advance refunding, for any lawful purpose, 
any Outstanding Bonds or Subordinated Indebtedness, where such refunding will not adversely 
affect the exclusion of the interest on any Tax-Exempt Bonds from gross income for the 
purposes of federal income tax. 
Upon the original issuance of Additional Bonds, the City must deliver to the Trustee 
certain certifications, including the following: 
(i) A Certificate of the Director of  Finance and the Director of Law, 
certifying that, to their knowledge, the City is  not, on the date of issuance of the Bonds, 
in default in the performance of any of its covenants provided in the General Bond 
Ordinance, in the Trust Agreement or in the Bonds; 
(ii) For any Series of Additional Bonds th at the City issues for the payment of 
Capital Costs or for the purpose of ref unding Subordinated Inde btedness or other 
obligations other than Outsta nding Bonds, either (A) a Cer tificate of the Director of 
Finance certifying that the Net Revenues Avai lable for Debt Service  for the preceding 
Fiscal Year or any consecutive 12 cal endar months during the 18-month period 
immediately preceding the date of original i ssuance of the proposed Series of Bonds (in 
each case, the “Test Period”) are in an amount not less than the greater of (1) 120% of 
maximum annual Debt Service on all Bonds then Outstanding and on the proposed Series 
of Additional Bonds or (2) 100% of the su m of: (A) maximum annual Debt Service on 
any Bonds then Outstanding and on the propos ed Series of Bonds, (B) all required 
deposits to the Debt Service Reserve Fund, (C ) all required deposits to the Subordinated 
Debt Service Fund and to any reserve fund securing Subordinated Indebtedness, (D) all  
B-24 
required deposits to the Contingency Fund, an d (E) debt service payable on any other 
obligations payable from the Balance Subfund and deposits to any reserve funds securing 
such other obligations, during that Test Period (the amo unts described in clauses (A) 
through (E) being referred to co llectively as the “Test Amount ”), or (B) a Certificate of 
the Director of Finance, which may be, but is not required to be, accompanied by or 
based upon a Certificate of a Consulting E ngineer, certifying that the Adjusted Net 
Revenues for the Test Period are in an amount  not less than the greater of (1) 120% of 
maximum annual Debt Service on any Bonds  then Outstanding and on the proposed 
Series of Bonds or (2) 100% of the Test Amount during that Test Period.  No certification 
under the provision described in this paragraph is required for any Series of Bonds being 
issued for the purpose of refunding Outstanding  Bonds, provided that  the issuance of the 
refunding Bonds will not result in any increase  in Debt Service in  any Fiscal Year; 
otherwise, the same certification is required as  for a Series of Bonds for the payment of 
Capital Costs; and 
For purposes of determining the City’s comp liance with the Additional Bonds Test, the 
amount of any Direct Payment received or expected  to be received by the C ity or the Trustee in 
any Fiscal Year will be credited against (i) Debt  Service in such Fiscal Year if such Direct 
Payment relates to Bonds or (ii) debt service on Subordinated Indebtedness in such Fiscal Year if 
such Direct Payment relates to Subordinated Indebtedness.  
For purposes of determining compliance with  the Rate Covenant and the Additional 
Bonds Test, the interest component of Debt Serv ice with respect to a Se ries of Bonds will be 
reduced by any accrued interest or  capitalized interest funded fr om the proceeds of Bonds, and, 
for the first annual period following the issuance of such Series of Bonds, will not include more 
than one year’s interest. 
Bond Anticipation Notes .  In anticipation of the issuan ce of any Series of Additional 
Bonds, the City may issue one or more Series of  Bond Anticipation Notes.  All requirements of 
the Trust Agreement applicable to Bonds also apply to Bond An ticipation Notes, including, 
without limitation the conditions precedent for the issuance of a Series of Bonds.  For the 
purpose of (i) determining compliance with the Rate  Covenant for any period prior to the date of 
calculation, (ii) determining whether Additional Bonds may be issued in compliance with the 
requirements with the Additional Bonds Te st when any Bond Anticipation Notes are 
outstanding, (iii) determining whether Bond Anticipation Notes may be issued in compliance 
with the requirements of the Additional Bonds Test, and (iv) determining the amount of the Debt 
Service Reserve Requirement attr ibutable to such B ond Anticipation Notes,  the Debt Service 
payable on any Bond Anticipation Notes will be computed for purposes of the Trust Agreement 
in accordance with in accordance with the provi sions of the Trust Agreement pertaining to 
Balloon Bonds and described in the subsection below entitled “Balloon Bonds.” 
Debt Service Reserve Requirement .  In connection with any issuance of Bonds, the City 
may, in the applicable Supplemen tal Trust Agreement, provide that no deposit to the Debt 
Service Reserve Fund will be made for or with re spect to such Additional Bonds, in which case:  
(i) the holders of such Additional Bonds will have  no right or entitlement to have any portion of 
the Bond Service Charges on such  Additional Bonds be paid from any amounts in the Debt 
Service Reserve Fund, (ii) the lien of and pl edge on the Debt Service Reserve Fund will not  
B-25 
extend to or be for the benefit of the holders of  such Bonds, and (iii) the Debt Service on such 
Bonds will not be taken into account in determining the Debt Service Reserve Requirement. 
In the event that the Supplemental Trust Agreement applicable to an issue of Additional 
Bonds provides as described in the preceding paragraph, then such Supplemental Trust 
Agreement may also provide for the creation of a special reserve account solely for such Bonds, 
separate from the Debt Service Reserve Fund, a nd may provide for the deposit therein, at the 
time of issuance or in one or more subsequent deposits thereto, of an amount specified in the 
applicable Supplemental Trust Agreement as the required reserve for such Bonds, or may require 
the City to provide a municipal bond insurance policy, a bank letter or line of credit, or any other 
form of credit or liquidity facility issued by a Qualified Financial Institution to enhance the 
security for such Bonds in lieu of a funded reserve account.  If the Supplemental Trust 
Agreement applicable to such a Series of Bonds so provides for such a special reserve account 
and further requires that deposits be made ther eto from Net Revenues at any time, then such 
deposits may be made only from moneys remain ing in the Revenue Fund on the last day of a 
month after any required deposits to the Debt Service Reserve Fund. 
If the Supplemental Trust Agreement applicab le to a Series of Bonds provides for no 
reserve account, or for a special reserve account as permitted by the preceding paragraph, then 
such Supplemental Trust Agreement must also  provide that the amount of any defaulted 
principal of or interest on such  Series of Bonds that would have  been timely paid had the Debt 
Service Reserve Requirement for such Bonds b een funded in the Debt Service Reserve Fund 
may be paid only from moneys remaining in th e Revenue Fund on the last day of a month after 
any required deposits to the Debt Service Reserve Fund. 
Computation of Debt Service With Respect to Bonds 
In the event that all or any portion of any Se ries of Bonds have been issued as or are 
proposed to be issued as Variab le Rate Bonds, then, except as ot herwise provided in the Trust 
Agreement, in order to compute the Debt Serv ice on such Bonds for the purposes of the Trust 
Agreement, the following rules will apply: 
Variable Rate Bonds.  Regarding Variable Rate Bonds: 
(i) For the purpose of determining comp liance with the Rate Covenant for 
any period prior to the date of calculation, the rate of interest borne by any Outstanding 
Variable Rate Bonds will be deemed to be the actual weighted average rate in effect 
thereon during such period. 
(ii) For the purpose of determini ng whether Bonds may be issued in 
compliance with the Additional Bonds Test, regardless of whether such Bonds are to be 
Variable Rate Bonds, the rate of interest to be borne by any Outstanding Variable Rate 
Bonds will be deemed to be the highest rate of interest borne by such Variable Rate 
Bonds during the preceding 24 m onths, but if such Variable Rate Bonds have not been 
outstanding for 24 months preceding the date of the computation, then it is to be assumed 
that such Variable Rate Bonds will bear interest at a fixed interest rate equal to 120% of 
the highest rate applicable within the 24 m onths immediately preceding the date of the 
computation under an index generally accepted in the securities i ndustry for securities  
B-26 
having ratings and maturity or tender date s comparable to those of the Outstanding 
Variable Rate Bonds. 
(iii) For the purpose of determining whethe r Bonds that are to be Variable Rate 
Bonds may be issued in compliance with th e Additional Bonds Test, and for the purpose 
of determining the amount of the Debt Servi ce Reserve Requirement, if any, attributable 
to such Variable Rate Bonds, the rate of interest to be borne by such Variable Rate Bonds 
will be deemed to be a fixed interest rate equal to 120% of the highest rate applicable 
within the 24 months immediately preceding the date of the computation under an index 
generally accepted in the securi ties industry for securities ha ving ratings and maturity or 
tender dates comparable to those of the proposed Variable Rate Bonds. 
(iv) For the purpose of determining wh ether any Outstanding Variable Rate 
Bond is deemed paid and discharged for purpos es of the Trust Agreement, such Variable 
Rate Bond will be deemed to bear interest at the actual rate of interest borne thereby for 
the remainder of the period that such rate remains in effect, and for any subsequent period 
prior to the date on which such Variable Rate Bond is actuall y to be paid and discharged, 
such Variable Rate Bond will be deemed to b ear interest at the maximum rate of interest 
such Variable Rate Bond may bear pursu ant to the Supplemental Trust Agreement 
applicable thereto. 
Balloon Bonds.  Regarding any Bonds that are or ar e proposed to be issued as Balloon 
Bonds, for the purpose of (i) determining complia nce with the Rate Covenant for any period 
prior to the date of calculation, (ii) determining whether Additional Bonds, regardless of whether 
they are to be Balloon Bonds, may be issued in compliance with the Additional Bonds Test when 
any Balloon Bonds are outstanding, (iii) determ ining whether Bonds that are to be Balloon 
Bonds may be issued in compliance with the A dditional Bonds Test, and (iv) determining the 
amount of the Debt Service Reserve Requirement, if any, attributable to such Balloon Bonds, the 
Debt Service on such Bonds will be determined as follows: 
(A) if such Balloon Bonds are not Capital Appreciation Bonds, by assuming 
that such Balloon Bonds are to be amortized on the basis of level debt service over the 
Assumed Amortization Period and that such Bonds  bear interest at the Assumed Interest 
Rate; and 
(B) if such Balloon Bonds are Capital Appreciation Bonds, by assuming that 
the Appreciated Principal Amount of such Bond s at maturity is to be amortized on the 
basis of level principal payments over the Assumed Amortization Period. 
Capital Appreciation Bonds.  Regarding any Bonds that are or are proposed to be issued 
as Capital Appreciation Bonds, for the purpose of (i) dete rmining compliance with the Rate 
Covenant for any period prior to the date of  calculation, (ii) determining whether Bonds, 
regardless of whether they are to be Capital Appreciation Bonds, may be issued in compliance 
with the Additional Bonds Test when any Cap ital Appreciation Bonds are outstanding, (iii) 
determining whether Bonds that are to be Ca pital Appreciation Bonds  may be issued in 
compliance with the Additional Bonds Test, and (iv) determining the amount of the Debt Service 
Reserve Requirement attributable to such Cap ital Appreciation Bonds, the Debt Service on such 
Bonds will include the Appreciated Principal Amounts at maturity.  
B-27 
Interest Rate Hedge Agreements .  If the City enters into an Interest Rate Hedge 
Agreement to simulate a fixed rate of interest on Variable Rate Bonds, then the City may (1) 
secure the portion of the payment obligations of the City thereunder that represents the 
equivalent of interest on the notional amount of  the Interest Rate Hedge Agreement with a 
pledge of the Net Revenues on a parity with the pledge thereof that secu res the Bonds, and (2) 
cause the debt structure that is simulated thr ough the combination of th e Variable Rate Bonds 
with such Interest Rate Hedge Agreement to ap ply for purposes of calcul ating or projecting the 
Debt Service on such Variable Rate Bonds for a ny period of time during which such Interest 
Rate Hedge Agreement is to be effective, provide d that (i) the debt structure that is simulated 
through the combination of the Variable Rate B onds with such Interest Rate Hedge Agreement 
complies with the restrictions of the Trust Agreem ent on the terms of and security for the Bonds 
applied to that structure as t hough it consisted entirely of Bonds and as though the portion of the 
payment obligations of the City thereunder that represents the equivalent of interest on the 
notional amount of the Interest Rate Hedge Agreement payable to the counterparty to the Interest 
Rate Hedge Agreement constituted Bond Service Charges, (ii) the count erparty to any swap 
agreement and the provider of any interest rate  cap is rated either of the two highest rating 
categories by at least two Rating Agencies, (iii) no such Interest Rate Hedge Agreement purports 
to entitle the counterparty to the Interest Rate Hedge Agreement to payment by the City from any 
source other than the Net Revenues, but such In terest Rate Hedge Agreement may provide for 
securing any portion of the paymen t obligations of the City thereunder that represents the 
equivalent of interest on the notional amount of the Interest Rate Hedge Agreement (but does not 
represent, among other things, any termination payment that may be payable by the City 
thereunder) with a pledge of th e Net Revenues on a parity with th e pledge thereof that secures 
the Bonds; and (iv) the cost of obtaining such  Interest Rate Hedge Agreement has been 
determined by the Director of Finance (who may obtain the written advice of a Financial 
Advisor) to be jus tified by the corresponding benefit to the City a nd to be commercially 
reasonable based on then current market conditions.  In the event the City enters into any such 
Interest Rate Hedge Agreement, it may not exercise any option to terminate such Interest Rate 
Hedge Agreement unless the Variable Rate Bonds to which such Interest Rate Hedge Agreement 
had related and that will remain outstanding after the termination thereof would fulfill the 
requirements of the Trust Agreement as they apply to Variable Rate Bonds, as though such 
Variable Rate Bonds were being issued on the da te of the termination of such Interest Rate 
Hedge Agreement.  If deposits to the Debt Service Fund for Parity Swap Obligations created 
pursuant this paragraph are required to be made more frequently than had been required for Bond 
Service Charges on any Outstanding Bonds, then, from and after the time such deposits for 
Parity Swap Obligations commence,  deposits to the Debt Service Fund must be required for all 
Outstanding Bonds with the same frequency as  they are required for such Parity Swap 
Obligations. 
If the City enters into an Interest Rate He dge Agreement to simulate a variable rate of 
interest on fixed rate Bonds, then  the City may (1) s ecure the portion of th e payment obligations 
of the City thereunder that re presents the equivalent of inte rest on the notiona l amount of the 
Interest Rate Hedge Agreement with a pledge of  the Net Revenues on a parity with the pledge 
thereof that secures the Bonds, and (2) cause the debt structur e that is simulated through the 
combination of the fixed rate Bonds with such Interest Rate Hedge Agreement to apply for 
purposes of calculating or projecting the Debt Service on such fixed rate Bonds for any period of 
time during which such Interest Rate Hedge Agreem ent is to be effective, provided that (i) the  
B-28 
debt structure that is simula ted through the combination of the fixed rate Bonds with such 
Interest Rate Hedge Agreement complies with the restrictions of the Trust Agreement on the 
terms of and security for the B onds applied to that structure as  though it consiste d entirely of 
Variable Rate Bonds and as though the portion of the payment obligations of the City thereunder 
that represents the equivalent of interest on the notional amount of the Interest Rate Hedge 
Agreement payable to the counterparty to the Interest Rate Hedge Agreement constituted Bond 
Service Charges, (ii) the counterparty to any swap agreement and the provider of any interest rate 
cap is rated either of the two highest rating cat egories by at least two Rating Agencies, (iii) no 
such Interest Rate Hedge Agreem ent purports to entitle the counterparty to the Interest Rate 
Hedge Agreement to payment by the City from any source other than the Net Revenues, but such 
Interest Rate Hedge Agreement may provide for securing any portion of the payment obligations 
of the City thereunder that re presents the equivalent of inte rest on the notiona l amount of the 
Interest Rate Hedge Agreement (but does not represent, among other things, any termination 
payment that may be payable by the City ther eunder) with a pledge of  the Net Revenues on a 
parity with the pledge thereof that secures the Bonds; and (iv) the cost of obtaining such Interest 
Rate Hedge Agreement has been determined by the Director of Finance (who may obtain the 
written advice of a financial advi sor) to be justified by the corresponding bene fit to the City and 
to be commercially reasonable based on then current market conditions.  In the event the City 
enters into any such Interest Rate Hedge Agreement, it may not exercise any option to terminate 
such Interest Rate Hedge Agreement unless the fixed rate Bonds to which such Interest Rate 
Hedge Agreement had related and that will remain outstanding after the termination thereof 
would fulfill the requirements of the Trust Agr eement as they apply to fixed rate Bonds, as 
though such fixed rate Bonds were being issued on the date of the termination of such Interest 
Rate Hedge Agreement.  If de posits to the Debt Service Fund for Parity Swap Obligations 
created pursuant this paragraph are required to be made more frequently than had been required 
for Bond Service Charges on any Outstanding Bonds, then, from and after the time such deposits 
for Parity Swap Obligations commence, deposits to the Debt Service F und must be required for 
all Outstanding Bonds with the same frequency as they are re quired for such Parity Swap 
Obligations. 
Covenants of the City 
The City covenants under the General Bond Or dinance with the Holders of the Bonds as 
follows: 
(i) The City will maintain the System , or will cause the System to be 
maintained, in sound operating condition and free from any liens or encumbrances which 
would interfere with the full and continuous use and operation thereof by the City. 
(ii) The City will keep proper books of record and account so as to show the 
complete financial results of the operati on of the System, including Revenues and 
Operating Expenses and all capital expenditures therefor, and will invest and deposit cash 
receipts that constitute Revenues in accordan ce with applicable laws, the General Bond 
Ordinance and the Trust Agreement. 
(iii) The City will at all times prescribe,  charge and collect such rates, rentals 
and other charges for the use of the services of the System and must restrict the Operating 
Expenses of the System in such a way th at Net Revenues Available for Debt Service  
B-29 
(adjusted for purposes of clause (i) as descri bed in the following sentence) in each Fiscal 
Year may be not less than the greater of (i) 120% of Debt Service on all Bonds then 
Outstanding payable during that Fiscal Year or (ii) 100% of the sum of: (A) Debt Service 
on all Bonds then Outstanding payable during th at Fiscal Year, (B) all required deposits 
to the Debt Service Reserve Fund during that Fi scal Year, (C) all required deposits to the 
Subordinated Debt Service Fund and to any reserve fund securing Subordinated 
Indebtedness during that Fiscal Year, (D) a ll required deposits to the Contingency Fund 
during that Fiscal Year, and (E) debt service payable on a ny other obligations payable 
from the Balance Subfund and deposits to any reserve funds securing such other 
obligations during that Fiscal Year.  For purpos es of clause (i) of the preceding sentence, 
but not for the purpose of clause (ii) of th e preceding sentence, “Net Revenues Available 
for Debt Service” for any Fiscal Year will in clude any amounts transferred from the Rate 
Stabilization Fund to the Revenue Fund during such Fiscal Year, but will be reduced by 
any amounts transferred from the Revenue F und to the Rate Stabilization Fund during 
that period.  For purposes of determining the City’s compliance with the Rate Covenant, 
the amount of any Direct Payments received by the City or the Trustee in any Fiscal Year 
will be credited against (i) Debt Service in such Fiscal Year if such Direct Payment 
related to Bonds or (ii) debt service on Subor dinated Indebtedness in such Fiscal Year if 
such Direct Payment related to Subordinated Indebtedness. 
(iv) If in any Fiscal Year the Net Reve nues Available for Debt Service is less 
than the amount required under paragraph (iii ), above, the City will, within 30 days 
following receipt by the City of its audited annual financial statement and the written 
request of the Trustee, employ a Consulting Engineer to make recommendations within 
45 days as to a revision of th e rates, fees and charges or Operating Expenses or methods 
of operation of the System, if any, that w ill result in producing the amount so required in 
the next succeeding Fiscal Year.  The City  covenants and agrees, promptly upon its 
receipt of such recommendations, to revise the rates, fees, and charges or Operating 
Expenses or methods of operation of the System  and to take such other action as is in 
conformity with such recommendations to the extent the City feasibly may do so and to 
notify the Trustee of the actions it has taken.  Upon the taking by the City of such actions, 
its failure to comply with the requirement described in paragraph (iii), above, will not 
constitute an Event of Default. 
(vi) The City will permit the authorized re presentative of the Trustee, or of any 
Holder or Holders of 25% of the aggregate principal amount of the Bonds at the time 
Outstanding, to inspect the System and all records, accounts, and data relating to 
Revenues and the collection thereof, at all reasonable times. 
(vii) The City will not create nor suffe r to be created any pledge, lien, or 
charge, except to secure Additional Bonds issued in accordance herewith, that would 
constitute a pledge or lien prior to, or on a parity with, the pledge of and lien on Net 
Revenues created by the General Bond Ordinance and the Trust Agreement to secure the 
Bonds. 
(viii) The City will main tain a risk management program that provides 
protection against risks of da mage or destruction of the System and liabilities for the 
operations of the System.  In furtherance thereof, the City may, among other things:  self- 
B-30 
insure in whole or in part; adopt alternative or supplemen tal risk management programs 
that the Council of the City determines to be  reasonable; organize either solely or in 
connection with other political subdivisi ons, organizations or captive insurance 
companies; participate in programs of captiv e insurance companies organized by others; 
establish a self-insurance trus t fund; participate in mutual or other cooperative insurance 
or other risk management programs or po ols with other political subdivisions or 
organizations; participate in or enter into agreements with local, State or federal 
governments in order to achieve such insurance;  or participate in other alternative risk 
management programs.  In case of any damage to or destruction of any part of the System 
amounting to a loss of $500,000 or more, the City promptly must give or cause to be 
given written notice thereof to the Trustee ge nerally describing the nature and extent of 
such damage or destruction.  Regardless of wh ether the net proceeds of insurance, if any, 
received on account of such damage or dest ruction are sufficient for such purpose, the 
City promptly will commence and complete, or cause to be commenced and completed, 
the repair or restoration of th e System as nearly as practicable to the value, condition and 
character thereof existing immediately prior to  such damage or dest ruction, with such 
changes or alterations, however, as the City  may deem necessary for proper operation of 
the System and as will not impair or diminis h, in the judgment of the City, the suitability 
of the System as a water pollution control system. 
(ix) The City will, for so long as any Bonds are Outstanding, retain under the 
control of the City all facilities from time  to time comprising the System, subject to 
disposition in the ordinary course for substitution or removal upon obsolescence, and 
will, in the exercise of such control, comply with all applicable requirements of law.  For 
purposes of the covenant desc ribed by this paragraph, the te rm “control” includes either 
the ownership or the operation of such facilities by the City. 
(x) The City will observe and perform all its agreements and obligations 
provided for by the Series 2016 Bonds, a ny Additional Bonds, the General Bond 
Ordinance or the Trust Agreement. 
(xi) The City will, for each Fiscal Ye ar, prepare and adopt, within the time 
period and in a manner prescribed by law,  a detailed budget of the estimated Revenues 
and Operating Expenses of the System.  The budget must provide for all operating 
Revenues, including interest income, and all Operating Expenses and other commitments 
required under the Trust Agreement. 
(xii) The City will take whatever actio n may be reasonably required to enforce 
its rights against any Person co llecting charges on be half of the City for the use of the 
System and to protect the City ’s interest in any funds colle cted by such Person that are 
payable to the City. 
Events of Default and Remedies 
The following constitute “Events of Default” under the Trust Agreement: 
(a) Default in the payment of any interest on any Bond when and as the same 
becomes due and payable;  
B-31 
(b) Default in the payment of the pr incipal of (including any Sinking Fund 
Installments) or any redemption premium on any Bond when and as the same becomes 
due and payable, whether at the stated matur ity or due date thereof, by acceleration or by 
call for redemption pursuant to any mandatory or optional redemption requirements; 
(c) Failure by the City to perform or observe any other covenant, agreement 
or condition on the part of the City cont ained in the General Bond Ordinance, any 
Supplemental Bond Ordinance, the Master Trust Agreement or any Supplemental Trust 
Agreement or in the Bonds (excep t if and to the extent that the City’s failure to perform 
or observe any such other covenant, agreement  or condition  is expressly stated not to 
constitute an Event of Default), which failure or default continues for a period of 60 days 
after written notice, by registered or certified mail, to the City specifying the failure or 
default and requiring the same to be remedied, which notice may be given by the Trustee 
in its discretion and which notice must be gi ven by the Trustee at th e written request of 
the Holders of not less than 25% in aggregate principal amount of Bonds then 
Outstanding; and 
(d) Certain acts of insolv ency involving the City. 
Upon the occurrence of an Event of Default described in paragraphs (a), (b) or (d) above, 
the Trustee may declare the principal of all Bonds then Outstanding (if not then due and payable) 
and the interest accrued thereon to be due a nd payable immediately, whereupon that portion of 
the principal of the Series 2016 Bonds thereby coming due and the interest thereon accrued to the 
date of payment will, without further action, become and be immediately due and payable, 
anything in the Trust Agreement or in the Series 2016 Bonds to the contrary notwithstanding.  If, 
after the occurrence of an Event of  Default, the principal and intere st has been thus declared due 
and payable because of such Event of Default, a nd prior to the entry of judgment in a court of 
law or equity for enforcem ent under the Trust Agreement or the appointment, and the 
confirmation thereof, of a receiver thereunder after an opportunity for hearing by the City, all 
sums payable under the Trust Agreement except the principal of, and intere st accrued after the 
next preceding Interest Payment Date on, the Bonds which have not reached their stated maturity 
dates and which are due and payable solely by reas on of that declaration, have been duly paid or 
provided for by deposit with the Trustee or Paying Agents, and all existing defaults have been 
made good, then and in every such case such pa yment or provision for payment will constitute a 
waiver of such Event of Default and its conse quences and an automatic recession and annulment 
of such declaration, but no such waiver and re scission will extend to or affect any such 
subsequent Event of Default or impair any rights consequent thereon. 
Upon the occurrence of any Event of Defau lt under the Trust Agreement, the Trustee, 
among other remedies, will be entitled to the appoin tment of a receiver to administer and operate 
the System on behalf of the City, upon the filing of  a suit to enforce the rights of the Trustee and 
the Holders of Bonds. 
Application of Moneys Received Pursuant to Remedial Action 
All moneys received by the Trustee or receiver pursuant to any right given or action 
taken under the provisions the Trust Agreement will first be applied to the payment of the cost 
and expenses of the proceedings resulting in th e collection of such moneys and of the fees,  
B-32 
expenses, liabilities and advances incurred or made by the Trustee or receiver.  The balance of 
such moneys will then be applied first to the pa yment, without priority or preference, of the 
interest on and principal or redemption premium of, if any, on the Bonds, in the manner set forth 
in the Trust Agreement. 
Rights and Remedies of Holders 
No Holder of any Bond will have any right to  institute any suit, action or proceeding for 
the enforcement of the Trust Agreement or for the execution of any trust thereof or for the 
appointment of a receiver or any other remedy under the Trust Ag reement unless an Event of 
Default has occurred and is continuing, such Hold er has previously have given to the Trustee 
written notice of such Event of  Default, and the Holders of not less than 25% in aggregate 
principal amount of Bonds then Outstanding have made written request to the Trustee and have 
afforded the Trustee reasonable opportunity either  to proceed to exercise the powers granted or 
to institute such action, suit or proceeding in its  own name and have also  offered to the Trustee 
an indemnity as provided in the Trust Agreement,  and the Trustee thereafter fails or refuses to 
exercise the powers granted under the Trust Agreem ent, or to institute such action, suit or 
proceeding in its own name. 
Rights and Remedies Related to Other Secured Obligations 
In connection with the City’s  entering into any Interest  Rate Hedge Agreement or 
Reimbursement Agreement or incurring or issuing any Subordinated Indebtedness, a 
Supplemental Trust Agreement may amend or s upplement the provisions of the Master Trust 
Agreement related to Events of Default and consequent rights and remedies to provide for the 
protection and enforcement of the ri ghts of the other party or partie s to such Interest Rate Hedge 
Agreement or Reimbursement Agreement or th e holder or holders of  such Subordinated 
Indebtedness and for the applic ation of moneys to the payment of Parity Swap Obligations, 
Credit Obligations or debt service charges on S ubordinated Indebtedness, provided that all such 
provisions must be consistent with the Master Trust Agreemen t and with the priorities of 
payment and security established hereby, and no such provision may diminish or derogate from 
the rights conferred on the Ho lders of Bonds and the priority  of Bond Service Charges in a 
manner inconsistent with those priorities.  Without  limiting the generality of the provision in the 
preceding sentence, no party entitled to the pa yment of Credit Obligations may be given the 
right, so long as any Bonds are outstanding or any Parity Swap Obligations are payable, to direct 
the acceleration of the maturity  of any Bonds, nor may the holders of any Subordinated 
Indebtedness be given the right, so long as any Bonds are outstanding or any Parity Swap 
Obligations or Credit Obligations are payable, to direct the acceleration of  the maturity of any 
Bonds.  The Trust Agreement provides that the provisions described in this paragraph will not be 
interpreted to limit the rights of Credit Providers to the enforcement of rights to payment of Bond 
Service Charges, nor may it be interpreted to limit the rights of parties entitled to the payment of 
Parity Swap Obligations to the enforcement of those rights.

any Rating Agency. 
All other Supplemental Trust Agreements must  be approved by the Holders of not less 
than 51% in aggregate principa l amount of the Bonds then out standing (excluding Bonds then

Defeasance 
If the City pays or causes to be paid all principal, redemption premium, if any, and 
interest due or to become due on the Bonds, and provision is made for paying all other sums 
payable by the City under the Trust Agreement, the Trustee will release and discharge the Trust 
Agreement.  All Outstanding Bonds will be deemed  to have been paid or caused to be paid 
within the meaning of the Trust Agreement if (i) the Trustee and any Paying Agents hold, in trust 
for and irrevocably committed thereto, sufficient moneys, or (ii) the Trustee will hold, in trust for 
and irrevocably committed thereto, Defeasance Obligations which are of such maturities and 
interest payment dates and bear such interest as will, without further investment or reinvestment 
of either the principal amount thereof or the inte rest earnings therefrom, be sufficient together 
with moneys referred to in clause (i) above, fo r the payment, at their maturity or redemption 
date, of all principal, redemption premium, if any, and interest thereof and thereon to the date of 
maturity or redemption, as the case may be, or if  default in such payment has occurred on such 
date then to the date of the tender of such payment; provided, that if any Bonds are to be 
redeemed prior to the maturity thereof, notice of  such redemption must have been duly given or 
provision satisfactory to the Trustee have been duly made for the giving of such notice. 
The Trustee 
The Trustee agrees in the Trust Agreement to  perform the trusts imposed upon it in the 
Trust Agreement as an ordinarily prudent truste e under a trust agreement.  The Trust Agreement 
provides that the Trustee may act upon the opinion or advice of any attorney and will not be 
responsible for any loss or damage resulting fr om any action taken or not taken in good faith 
reliance upon such opinion or advice.  In addition, the Trust Agreement provides that the Trustee 
will be protected in acting upon certain documents believed to be genuine and correct and to 
have been signed or sent by the proper persons. 
Extent of City’s Covenants; No Personal Liability 
All covenants, stipulations, obligations and agreements of the City contained in the Trust 
Agreement will be deemed to be covenants, stipulations, obligations and agreements of the City 
to the full extent authorized by the Ohio Revised Code and permitted by the Constitution of the 
State and the Charter of the City.  No covenant, stipulation, obligation or agreement contained in 
the Trust Agreement will be deemed to be a covenant, stipulation, obligation or agreement of any 
present or future member of the Council of the City or agent or employee of the City in his or her 
individual capacity, and neither the members of the Council of the City nor any official 
executing the Bonds will be liable personally on the B onds or be subject to any personal liability 
or accountability by reason of the issuance thereof.

FORM OF BOND COUNSEL OPINION 
April 14, 2016 
To: City of Cleveland, Ohio 
 Morgan Stanley & Co. LLC 
            Zions Bank, a Division of ZB, National Association, as Trustee 
We have served as bond counsel to our client the City of Cleveland, Ohio (the “City”), and 
not as counsel to any other person in connect ion with the issuance by the City of its $32,390,000 
Water Pollution Control Revenue Bonds, Series 2016 (the “Series 2016 Bonds”), dated the date 
of this letter.  The Series 2016 Bonds are issued pursuant to the authority of the Constitution and 
laws of the State of Ohio, including Article XV III of the Ohio Constitu tion, the Charter of the 
City, and Ordinances No. 29-16 (the “General  Bond Ordinance”) and No. 28-16 (the “Series 
2016 Ordinance”), each passed by the Council of  the City on January 25, 2016, and under the 
Master Trust Agreement, dated April 14, 2016,  which includes the General Bond Ordinance 
(together, the “Master Trust Agreement”), as  supplemented by the First Supplemental Trust 
Agreement, dated April 14, 2016, which include s the Series 2016 Ordinance (the “First 
Supplemental Trust Agreement” and together with the Master Trust Agreement, the “Trust 
Agreement”), each between the City and Zions Bank, a Division of ZB, Na tional Association, as 
trustee (the “Trustee”).  Capitalized terms not otherwise defined in this letter are used as defined 
in the Trust Agreement. 
 
In our capacity as bond counsel, we have examin ed the transcript of proceedings relating 
to the issuance of the Series 2016 Bonds, a c opy of the signed and authenticated Series 2016 
Bond of the first maturity, the Trust Agreement and such other documents, matters and laws as 
we deem necessary to render the opinions set forth in this letter. 
 
Based on that examination and subject to the limitations stated below, we are of the 
opinion that under existing law:  
 
1. The Series 2016 Bonds a nd the Trust Agreement are valid and binding obligations of 
the City enforceable in accordance with their respective terms. 
 
2. The Series 2016 Bonds constitute special obligations of the City, and the principal 
of and interest (collectively, “debt se rvice”) on the Series 2016 Bonds, together 
with debt service on Bonds to be issued and outstanding, from time to time, under 
the Master Trust Agreement (collectivel y, the “Bonds”), are payable from and 
secured solely by the Net Revenues a nd Special Funds established under the 
Master Trust Agreement, all as described in the Trust Agreement.  The Bonds and 
the payment of debt service on the B onds are not secured by an obligation or 
pledge of any money raised by taxa tion, and the Bonds do not represent or  
C-2 
constitute a general obligati on debt of the City or a pl edge of the fa ith and credit 
of the City, the State of Ohio or any of its political subdivisions. 
 
3. Interest on the Series 2016 Bonds is excluded from gross income for federal income 
tax purposes under Section 103 of the Internal Revenue Code of 1986, as amended 
(the “Code”), and is not an item of tax preference for purpos es of the federal 
alternative minimum tax imposed on individuals an d corporations; however, 
portions of the interest on the Series 2016 Bonds earned by certain corporations may 
be subject to a corporate alternative minimum tax.  Interest on, and any profit made 
on the sale, exchange or other disposition of, the Series 2016 Bonds are exempt from 
all Ohio state and local ta xation, except the estate tax, the domestic insurance 
company tax, the dealers in intangibles tax, the tax levied on the basis of the total 
equity capital of financial institutions, and the net wo rth base of the corporate 
franchise tax.  We express no opinion as to any other tax consequences regarding the 
Series 2016 Bonds. 
 
The opinions stated above are based on an analysis of existing laws , regulations, rulings 
and court decisions and cover certain matters not directly addressed by such authorities.  In 
rendering all such opinions we assume, without independent verification, and rely upon (i) the 
accuracy of the factual matters represented, warranted or certified in the proceedings and 
documents we have examined, (ii) the due and legal authorization, ex ecution and delivery of 
those documents by, and the valid, binding and enforceable nature of those documents upon, any 
parties other than the City, and (iii) the due  authorization, signing and delivery by, and the 
binding effect upon and enforceability against, the Trustee of the Trust Agreement. 
 
In rendering those opinions with respect to the treatment of the interest on the Series 2016 
Bonds under the federal tax laws, we further assume and rely upon compliance with the covenants 
in the proceedings and documents we have exam ined, including those of the City.  Failure to 
comply with certain of those covenants subse quent to issuance of th e Series 2016 Bonds may 
cause interest on th e Series 2016 Bonds to be included in gross income for federal income tax 
purposes retroactively to their date of issuance. 
 
The rights of the owners of the Series 2016 Bonds and the enforceability of the Series 
2016 Bonds and the Trust Agreement are subject  to bankruptcy, insolvency, arrangement, 
fraudulent conveyance or transfer, reorganizati on, moratorium and other laws relating to or 
affecting creditors’ rights, to the application of e quitable principles, to the exercise of judicial 
discretion, and to limitations on legal remedies against public entities. 
 
The opinions rendered in this letter are stated  only as of this date, and no other opinion 
shall be implied or inferred as a result of anythi ng contained in or omitted from this letter.  Our 
engagement as bond counsel with respect to the Series 2016 Bonds has concluded on this date. 
Respectfully submitted,
